onDefinition
function fzf-recent-dirs
    get_recent_dirs | __fzf_helper_cmd
end


function __fzf_helper_cmd
    set -l preview_cmd 'exa -F --sort=changed --reverse --icons --git-ignore {}'
    fzf --tiebreak=index --preview "$preview_cmd" --preview-window=right:60%:wrap "$_FZF_NAV_KEYS" 
end

Instead, we use the same hack as __fish_complete_subcommand and\n\t# extract the subcommand manually.\n\tset -l cmd (commandline -co) (commandline -ct)\n\tswitch $cmd[1]\n\t\tcase env sudo\n\t\t\tfor i in (seq 2 (count $cmd))\n\t\t\t\tswitch $cmd[$i]\n\t\t\t\t\tcase '-*'\n\t\t\t\t\tcase '*=*'\n\t\t\t\t\tcase '*'\n\t\t\t\t\t\tset cmd $cmd[$i..-1]\n\t\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t\tend\n\t\t\tend\n\tend\n        set cmd (string join -- ' ' $cmd)\n\n\tset -l complist (complete -C$cmd)\n\tset -l result\n        #string join -- \\n $complist | sort | eval (__fzfcmd) -m --select-1 --exit-0 --header '(commandline)' | cut -f1 | while read -l r; set result $result $r; end\n        string join -- \\n $complist | sort | fzf -m --select-1 --exit-0 --header '(commandline)' | cut -f1 | while read -l r; set result $result $r; end \n\tset prefix (string sub -s 1 -l 1 -- (commandline -t))\n\tfor i in (seq (count $result))\n\t\tset -l r $result[$i]\n\t\tswitch $prefix\n\t\t\tcase \"'\"\n\t\t\t\tcommandline -t -- (string escape -- $r)\n\t\t\tcase '\"'\n\t\t\t\tif string match '*\"*' -- $r >/dev/null\n\t\t\t\t\tcommandline -t --  (string escape -- $r)\n\t\t\t\telse\n\t\t\t\t\tcommandline -t -- '\"'$r'\"'\n\t\t\t\tend\n\t\t\tcase '~'\n\t\t\t\tcommandline -t -- (string sub -s 2 (string escape -n -- $r))\n\t\t\tcase '*'\n\t\t\t\tcommandline -t -- (string escape -n -- $r)\n\t\tend\n\t\t[ $i -lt (count $result) ]; and commandline -i ' '\n\tend\n\n\tcommandline -f repaint\nend\n"

Example below.\n#                       $argv                            preview\n#                  ____________________________________________________\n#                       ~/.config/nvim/init.vim  |    bat ~/.config/nvim/init.vim\n#                       ~/.config/nvim/          |    ls ~/.config/nvim/\n#                       nvim                     |    man nvim\n#\nfunction __print_preview_cmd_1\n    if test -d $HOME/$argv\n        set -U EXA_COLORS (vivid generate exa_theme)\n        exa --icons $HOME/$argv\n    else if test -d $argv\n        set -U EXA_COLORS (vivid generate exa_theme)\n        exa --icons $argv\n    else if test -f $HOME/$argv\n        bat-fzf-helper $HOME/$argv\n    else if test -f $argv\n        bat-fzf-helper $argv\n    else if type -q $argv\n        if type -fq $argv\n            man -a $argv 2> /dev/null | sed '/troff.*$/d' | bat-fzf-helper\n            #man $argv | batcat | grep --invert-match \"troff\";\n        else \n            bat-fzf-helper (functions -D $argv 2> /dev/null)\n        end\n    else \n        set -l dir (dirname $argv)\n        if test -d .git\n            git show $argv;\n        else if test -d $dir/.git\n            git show $argv;\n        else if test -d $dir;\n            exa --icons $dir;\n        else if test -d $HOME/$dir\n            exa --icons $HOME/$dir;\n        else\n            spaced_print_seperator;\n            set_random_color; echo \"UNSURE OF $argv\";\n            spaced_print_seperator;\n            set_random_color; echo \"Potential commands:\";\n            set_random_color; type -pa $argv;\n            spaced_print_seperator;\n        end\n    end\nend\n\n# __print_preview_cmd_2 - Prints the preview of the command\n# when there is an argument included. History function of fzf\n# will show results for commands that are not just a single ft/dir/man page.\n#\n# @param argv - array of $argv initially passed to _fzf_preview. Example below.\n#               \n#     command in _fzf_preview     cd ~/.config\n#     argv index                  [1]  [2]\n#\nfunction __print_preview_cmd_2\n    set -l cmd $argv[1]\n    set -l arg (string replace -r \"[.]+/\" \"\" \"$argv[2]\")\n    if test -d $HOME/$arg; or test -d $arg\n        __print_preview_cmd_1 $arg;\n    else if test -f $HOME/$arg; or test -f $arg\n        __print_preview_cmd_1 $arg;\n    else \n        # check for cmd to be of some recognized type\n        # correlating to a file or directory\n        if test $cmd = \"cd\"\n            __find_from_home_directory 1 $arg\n        else if test $cmd = \"nvim\"\n            __find_from_home_directory 0 $arg\n        else \n            __display_initial_param $argv\n        end\n    end\nend\n\n# __print_preview_cmd_3 - Prints the preview of the command\n# when there is an argument included. History function of fzf\n# will show results for commands that are not just a single ft/dir/man page.\n#\n# @param argv - array of $argv initially passed to _fzf_preview. Example below.\n#               \n#     command in _fzf_preview     cd ~/.config\n#     argv index                  [1]  [2]\n#\nfunction __print_preview_cmd_3\n    __display_initial_param $argv\n    set -l cmd $argv[1]\n    set -l arg $argv[2]\n    set -l remaining $argv[3..]\n    print_seperator;\n    echo \"\"($cmd --help);\n    print_seperator;\n    set -l found_pipe false\n    for f_d in $remaining\n        if string match -qae -- \"echo\" \"$fd\"\n            set found_pipe false\n            continue;\n        else if string match -qae -- \"-\" \"$f_d\"\n            set found_pipe false\n            continue;\n        else if string match -qae -- \"|\" \"$f_d\"\n            set found_pipe true;\n            continue;\n        else if test $found_pipe \n            __print_preview_cmd_1 $f_d\n            set found_pipe false\n        end\n    end\nend\n\n\n# __find_from_home_directory - Finds the file or directory\n# from the home directory.\n#\n# @param is_dir - boolean value to determine if the file is a directory\n# @param name - the name of the file or directory\n#\nfunction __find_from_home_directory \n    set -l is_dir $argv[1]\n    set -l name $argv[2]\n    set -l found\n    echo \"$is_dir\"\n    if test $is_dir -eq 0\n        set found (fd -a --base-directory \"$HOME\" --type f --hidden --glob \"$name\")\n    else\n        set found (fd -a --base-directory \"$name\" --type d --hidden)\n    end\n    for item in $found\n        if test -d $item\n            lst $item\n        else\n            bat-fzf-helper $item;\n        end\n    end\nend\n\n# __display_initial_param - Prints the initial preview of the command\n#\n# @param argv - $argv passed to _fzf_preview. Example below.\n#\n#               _________________________\n#               $argv\n#               _________________________\n#\nfunction __display_initial_param\n    set_color normal; print_seperator;\n    set_random_color; echo \"$argv\"; \n    set_color normal; print_seperator;\nend\n"

function fzf-dir-preview
    set -l dir (string replace -r --all '~' "$HOME" "$argv")
    exa --sort=changed --reverse --icons $dir 
    if test -d "$dir"
        exa --sort=changed --reverse --icons $dir
    else 
        error_text "EXA ERROR: "
        echo -n "'$dir'"
        error_text " is not a valid directory"
    end
end

function error_text
        set_color red --bold
        echo -n "$argv"
        set_color normal --background normal
end
